H Action Required: FYI ESE. seh. |

i. Forwarded under separate cover is an issue of a |
supposedly "literary" Cuban publication containing two short
essays by the Salvadorian poet and writer Roque DALTON. |
The first of these essays is dedicated to LIRING-3. The ~
interesting thing is that LIRING~3 was at that time imprisoned
in Guatemala. The essay may thus be viewed as a tribute to

“a Sulie®icg supporter ox the cause."

2, Roque DALTON (201-215097) is, according to the files
of the Station, an agent of the Cuban Intelligence Service’
engaged in clandestine activities for the Communist Party of
El Salvador. DALTON spent some time in Czechoslovakia and is
now living in Cuba. He is the brother of Margarita DALTON
(201-751261), whom the Cuban IS recruited to work in VWexico.
LIRING-3 got to know DALTON in Havana in 1962-63 and became
a close friend of his (see HMMA-32283, 19 June 1967). DALTON
at one point confided to LIRING-3 that he had been approached
by WOFIRM while incarcerated in El Salvador. ;

{

3. The Station is hoping that DALTON's essay is an [|
indication that LIRING-3 is going to be viewed by the Cubans
in much better light after his incarceration in Guatemala. |
A report of LIRING-3's complete debriefing by ROWTON was
forwarded with HMMA-35904, 27 November 1968.

La palma do ti mane sobre el rio.

Lu palma paso a paso, hacia mi, leyéndome.
Warciso muascado por la nicbla ascendente,
vuelven los dioses desvensores, Orfeo

Y Stephanopherophoro.

EL Indice demuestea. sefala la inflexible
Jimura dei teve, denitonteay

AEE tndice demuestra ta carreta sobre un hilo,
Ja dingenal con cuerpo de cocadrile

y eabean de gavilan,

eb anitio de oro en el tumor de ta luna.

Ta mano se exticnde sobre Ia Hanura

de nieve, la pahna de la mano

acompasa la boga del rio.

La carreta conduce un canoso

reloj de pared. Iearo con dos guadaiias.
Saturno se come las alas de cora,

Se extiende, demuestra, se deja leor,

Tearo, ya ealdo, nadando,

habla con cl Resucitndo sentado en el kégamo.
EL vencida por el sal regresa con las estaclones
y cl que triunfa de Ia muerte se vuelve a morir,
Fis un boderda de cebotla, mangana y anapolas,
exprimide en eb pu

eb arador por kt palma de la mano
deja el reminiscente batido y batihojas,
el deseo paliducho, la scrpiente, el doble
del comicnzo, el truchiman vi
efreulo que yzolpea ca ins 1 OS.

La capota caida se mide por su sonbra,
Iearo vencide y el Resucitado veneedor,
el Resucitado esperando la muerte

y el Icaro eterno relator.

En su sanpre el laberinto y cl torete
oscuro luchando con cl tigre dormido,

que se ¢
